<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;7.01 Regulation&nbsp;FD Disclosure</B>


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">On December&nbsp;16, 2004, Federal Signal Corporation (the &#147;Registrant&#148;) held a conference call to
discuss progress with restructuring initiatives and the outlook for 2005. A copy of the
presentation materials and the discussion script is attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">The information in this Current Report is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the
purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to
the liabilities of that Section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated
by reference into any registration statement or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of
1933, as amended.

<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">Robert D. Welding, President and Chief Executive Officer:

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD>Good morning everyone and thank you for joining us. I&#146;d like to welcome you to our
2005 Outlook conference call.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Joining me is Stephanie Kushner, our CFO. She will be available to answer questions
with me after some prepared remarks.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

what has taken place to-date and what you can expect in the near future.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

</TR>

performance measurement system into our business, and aligning incentive systems more
directly with shareholder interests.</TD>
</TR>

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<!-- Slide Number 0004 -->
<CENTER>
<IMG src="c90671c906711z0004.gif" alt="(POWERPOINT SLIDE)">
</CENTER>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This chart shows the status of the restructuring initiatives we announced at the end of
June. At the time we specifically identified 7 transactions and indicated that beyond
those, a few businesses that we had determined to be non-core would be divested over time,
if we could get fair price.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>With the recovery in the industrial sector this year, it has proven to be a seller&#146;s
market and we closed on two businesses in December per our recent announcements. We have
one more in the works that we think will close in the first quarter of next year.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In these three cases we were able to realize proceeds that were near or at the Net
Present Value of the future Economic Value of the businesses.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Before continuing, I&#146;d like to take a moment to express my appreciation to the
employees of all of the businesses we have divested during the past months for their
loyalty and great performance during the years Federal Signal operated the businesses, and
during the unnerving due diligence process. We wish all of them continued success in
their new corporate families.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This list of transactions represents the first step in our strategy to position
ourselves to aggressively create shareholder value in the coming years, and over the long
term. We will have shrunk by some $100&nbsp;million in revenue, but in doing so, we have
narrowed the focus of our resources to concentrate on those core products and businesses
that will carry us into a more profitable future.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Several months ago I told you that our operating structure was excessively complex for
a company our size. We were operating 52 plants in 35 separate locations. With the
completion of these restructuring and divestiture activities, we will have reduced our
operating footprint by 13 separate locations, or by 1/3. This will improve our fixed cost
picture as we move forward as a leaner more focused organization.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Even with these divestitures, our revenue for 2005 will be about $1.2&nbsp;billion,
essentially equal to 2004.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>As we&#146;ve indicated, our objective over the long-term is to grow the top line at a rate
in the high single digits, so we&#146;re off to a decent start &#151; net of the divestitures. I
will reiterate that it is our intention to achieve 2/3 of this growth organically, and the
remainder through acquisitions, roughly speaking.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<TABLE width="90%">
<TR><TD><FONT size="1" color="#FFFFFF" style="font-size: 1pt; color: #FFFFFF">

   Transactions   Status

   Sale of Kelowna production facility in British Columbia    Completed

   Divestiture of taxable leasing portfolio   Completed
   Cease Mfg Operations at Dayton France    Completed
   Sale of Technical Tooling, Inc.   Completed

<!-- Slide Number 0005 -->
<CENTER>
<IMG src="c90671c906711z0005.gif" alt="(POWERPOINT SLIDE)">
</CENTER>




<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Most of our restructuring activity during the past 6&nbsp;months was directed at our two
troubled businesses &#151; Fire Rescue and Refuse</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We have much of the heavy lifting behind us, except for transitioning production of
rear-loader refuse bodies to Medicine Hat, which will occur in the first quarter of next
year. Of course we will still have a lot of work to do to get all of the wrinkles ironed
out after that, but we&#146;re hoping we&#146;ll be in pretty good shape by about mid-way through
the second half of the year.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In regard to the Preble fire truck plant closure, as of a few weeks ago we began
production of stainless-steel bodies in our Ocala facility and production at Preble will
cease at the end of this month. As announced previously, we have restricted orders for
stainless-steel trucks during most of the past year to result in a backlog where we could
concentrate on a smaller number of pre-configured models as we climb up the learning curve
in Ocala. We have made only 40 production slots available during 2005 for stainless-steel
trucks, down from a normal 100. We will expand to include a full offering again down the
road, but will turn our backs on those ultra-complex vehicles, way-out at the end of the
curve, that we would have taken on in the past.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>This is not to suggest we are changing our business model, we will still be in the very
highly customized fire apparatus business offering at least as many options as our major
competitors. But we are structuring the cab and body designs into modular components so
we can improve our efficiency, lead-time, and quality. The configurator tool we are
implementing is facilitating this.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="90%">
<TR><TD><FONT size="1" color="#FFFFFF" style="font-size: 1pt; color: #FFFFFF">

Focus of Restructuring

Environmental Products Group

Divested components manufacturing plant in
Kelowna (British Columbia)

Closing Oshkosh (WI) Refuse truck plant and
consolidating operations into Medicine Hat (Alberta)

Fire Rescue Group

Divested Plastisol J.V. in the Netherlands

Closing Preble (NY) plant and consolidating
operations into Ocala (FL)

Phasing out assembly operation in the Netherlands
early in 2005 after completion of RNLAF project

</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

projects

Growth in profitable product lines

Divestiture of non-core
businesses
      2005   Longer Term
   Safety Products Group

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Our Tool Group revenue growth is less spectacular with our growth rate in the U.S.
moderating slightly, reflecting a comfortable but less robust GNP growth rate.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We see some recovery in Germany which has been very weak for most of 2004, although
France softens further in 2005.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>After a nice increase in Japan during 2004 as we introduced a new product line into the
market, we see that region leveling off.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Margins continue to improve as we see the benefits of the restructuring moves in 2003
and 2004, our ERP problems behind us, and continuing attention being paid to improve
efficiency.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Beyond 2005, we will continue to expand in growing regions outside of our traditional
markets.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="90%">
<TR><TD><FONT size="1" color="#FFFFFF" style="font-size: 1pt; color: #FFFFFF">

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<!-- Slide Number 0013 -->
<CENTER>
<IMG src="c90671c906711z0013.gif" alt="(POWERPOINT SLIDE)">
</CENTER>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>When I joined Federal Signal a little over a year ago, I set out to help transform
a good business that was struggling, into a great business that generates impressive
shareholder value over a sustained period.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In order to do this I knew I had to make some significant changes, not only to our
business portfolio, but also in how we motivate and compensate our employees.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>I am very excited to announce that, after much design work and training, our EV
measurement system is ready to be rolled out in January of 2005.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We will start by basing the variable compensation of our top four layers of management
directly to specific EV targets. The rest of our employees will be tied to EV in some
capacity as well, as we roll this out throughout the organization over the next couple of
years.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The targets that we have established are consistent with the kind of profitable growth
I&#146;ve outlined this morning. A notable feature is that we&#146;ve set the targets for the next
three years which will eliminate the practice of negotiating bonus targets around a budget
each year.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We also have a provision that allows a missed bonus one year to be recovered over the
next two years if EV performance gets back on track. This will encourage our people to
make good investments for the long term, even if it impacts their compensation in the
short-term.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Our Board is in the process of reviewing the compensation design for various layers of
our salaried workforce. There is a realization that we need to get more Federal Signal
shares into the hands of our top management people, again to more directly align their
interests with those of our
shareholders. We will likely have a proposal along these lines in our Proxy in 2005.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="90%">
<TR><TD><FONT size="1" color="#FFFFFF" style="font-size: 1pt; color: #FFFFFF">

Economic Value (EV)

Economic Value (EV) measurement system will be
incorporated effective January 2005

Variable compensation of top 240 employees (top four
layers of management) will be 100% based on EV

EV target goals are in alignment with the revenue growth
and operating margin guidance provided earlier

Bonus system has targets set for the next three years and
has a two-year carry forward provision to accommodate
good long-term investment opportunities



</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<!-- Slide Number 0014 -->
<CENTER>
<IMG src="c90671c906711z0014.gif" alt="(POWERPOINT SLIDE)">
</CENTER>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In summary, we are working to transform this company to one with top line sales
growth in the range of 8-10% per annum. We expect two thirds of this growth to be
organic, with the balance coming from <U>focused</U> acquisitions that build on our core
products. More growth will be overseas than domestic, with a bias toward expansion in
Asia.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We expect to reverse the erosion trend on our operating margins and target 10% as being
good performance for our mix of businesses. We will do this through increased focus on
material sourcing, lowering our fixed costs through plant consolidations, continuing our
implementation of Lean principles, and better focusing our SG&#038;A spend, using shared
back-office processing centers.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>We will improve our return on invested capital.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>

    <TD>In 2005, we should experience a significant improvement due to the impact of
restructuring initiatives.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="2%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>

    <TD>Beyond 2005, our goal will be to improve returns by at least 1% per annum.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="left">&#149;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>And we have set an EV compensation target that gets us to a positive EV by the end of
2007.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="90%">
<TR><TD><FONT size="1" color="#FFFFFF" style="font-size: 1pt; color: #FFFFFF">

Vision for Federal Signal

Sales Growth - 8-10%

Operating Margins ~10%

Improving ROIC

2005:  Restructuring Impact

2006+: min 1% per year

Positive Economic Value by 2007
</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
